PolicyAuditLogger provides structured logging of policy evaluation decisions\n// for audit and debugging purposes.\ntype PolicyAuditLogger struct {\n\tlock.Mutex\n\n\tlogger *slog.Logger\n\tlevel  slog.Level\n\toutput io.Writer\n}\n\n// NewPolicyAuditLogger creates a new PolicyAuditLogger with the specified logger,\n// log level, and output destination.\nfunc NewPolicyAuditLogger(logger *slog.Logger, level slog.Level, output io.Writer) *PolicyAuditLogger {\n\tif logger == nil {\n\t\tlogger = slog.New(slog.NewTextHandler(output, &slog.HandlerOptions{Level: level}))\n\t}\n\treturn &PolicyAuditLogger{\n\t\tlogger: logger,\n\t\tlevel:  level,\n\t\toutput: output,\n\t}\n}\n\n// LogDecision logs a policy decision with the given identity, policy, verdict, and reason.\n// This method reason,\n\t)\n}\n\n// EvaluationResult represents the result of a policy evaluation.\ntype EvaluationResult struct {\n\tAllowed bool\n\tDenied  bool\n\tError   error\n}\n\n// LogEvaluation logs a policyKey,\n\t\t\"allowed\", result.Allowed,\n\t\t\"denied\", result.Denied,\n\t}\n\n\tif result.Error != nil {\n\t\tattrs = append(attrs, logfields.Error, result.Error)\n\t}\n\n\tif selectorCache != nil {\n\t\tstats := selectorCache.Stats()\n\t\tattrs = append(attrs, \"selectors\", stats.selectors, \"identities\", stats.identities)\n\t}\n\n\tpal.logger.Log(ctx, pal.level, \"policy evaluation\",\n\t\tattrs...,\n\t)\n}\n\n// SetLevel sets the log level for the audit logger.\n// This method is thread-safe.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) SetLevel(level slog.Level) slog.Level\n\toutput io.Writer\n}\n\n// NewPolicyAuditLogger creates a new PolicyAuditLogger with the specified logger,\n// log level, and output destination.\nfunc NewPolicyAuditLogger(logger
